
namespace = PlusFaction

#reserved: PlusFaction.100 to PlusFaction.299

############################################
# MEETING EVENTS FOR ALL REGULAR FACTIONS
############################################

### CALLING THE MEETING

# Faction leader convenes a meeting
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.100
	picture = "GFX_evt_emissary"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_100"
	
	only_rulers = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		NOT = { trait = neutral }
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed }
			had_character_flag = {
				flag = faction_meeting_postponed
				days = 730
			}
			AND = {
				had_character_flag = {
					flag = faction_meeting_postponed
					days = 365
				}
				NOT = {
					liege = {
						any_war = {
							defender = {
								character = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting }
			had_character_flag = {
				flag = faction_meeting
				days = 1095
			}
			AND = {
				had_character_flag = {
					flag = faction_meeting
					days = 730
				}
				NOT = {
					liege = {
						any_war = {
							defender = {
								character = PREVPREV
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry 
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
					in_faction = faction_republican_king
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
					in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
					in_faction = faction_religious_king
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
					in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
					in_faction = faction_court_king
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
					in_faction = faction_court_duke
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
			}
		}
		had_global_flag = { flag = startup days = 730 }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting_called }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.05
			OR = {
				has_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
				had_character_flag = {
					flag = faction_meeting
					days = 2555
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			NOT = {
				liege = {
					any_war = {
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry 
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_court_angry 
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry 
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry 
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_100" #Send out the invitations
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
			set_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 0 }
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP51 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP52 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP53 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP54 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.102 }
			}
			character_event = { id = PlusFaction.105 days = 7 } # regular meeting
			character_event = { id = PlusFaction.106 days = 7 } # angry meeting
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_100" #It can wait
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 0.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 2.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 3.5 }
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP50 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 0.5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1.5 } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 33
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.101 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1.5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 2.5 } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.101 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 2.5 }
				NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 3.5 } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.101 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 3.5 }
			}
			character_event = { id = PlusFaction.101 tooltip = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_meeting_delay" value = 1 } }
	}
}

# Faction leader replaced due to postponing the meeting for too long
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.101
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_101"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.125 } #notify
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
		set_character_flag = removed_from_leadership
	}

	option = {
		name = "CURSES"
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -400
		}
	}
}

# Faction member receives the invitation to the meeting
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.102
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_102"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_102" #I will attend
	}
}

# Regular meeting - setting the agenda
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.105
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_105"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes
	
	only_rulers = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
		has_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		NOT = { trait = neutral }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					liege = {
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
					in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
					in_faction = faction_republican_king
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
					in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
					in_faction = faction_religious_king
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
					in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
					in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
					in_faction = faction_court_king
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
				AND = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
					in_faction = faction_court_duke
					higher_tier_than = BARON
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge_defeated
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_105" #I will strengthen my position within the faction
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = content
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = charitable
			}
		}
		character_event = { id = PlusFaction.130 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900600 } #strengthen own position
		clr_character_flag = prevent_ai_loop
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_105" #I plan to rally support for my liege
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}

			}
		}
		character_event = { id = PlusFaction.132 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900602 } #weaken liege
		clr_character_flag = prevent_ai_loop
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTE_PlusFaction_106" #We are not strong enough to act yet
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				liege = {
					any_war = {
						defender = {
							character = PREVPREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.49 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } } }
			}
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP57 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 0.74 } }
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 0.99 } } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.120 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 0.99 } }
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.49 } } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.120 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.49 } }
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } } }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.120 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.120 } }
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
		clr_character_flag = prevent_ai_loop
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTF_PlusFaction_106" #Now is not the time to act
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP59 }
		trigger = {
			liege = {
				any_war = {
					defender = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
						leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_court_king
						leads_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_religious_king
						leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
					}
				}
				AND = {
					OR = {
						leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						leads_faction = faction_republican_king
						leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					liege = {
						has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
		clr_character_flag = prevent_ai_loop
	}
}

### REACTIONS TO LIEGE AGREEING/REFUSING DEMANDS

# Liege has refused demands to lower crown authority
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.110 #formerly 1000182471
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_110"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_110" #Then we go to war!
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
				leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_religious_king
				leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_republican_king
				leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_court_king
				leads_faction = faction_court_duke
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 0.49 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 0.74 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.49 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5.0
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100.0
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 2.99 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.204 } #vote
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
				change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
				change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 4 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { real_tier = KING }
				change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 8 }
			}
		}
		character_event = { id = PlusFaction.172 days = 7 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900737 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_110" #Do nothing
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.49 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = count
				}
				prestige = -25
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = duke
				}
				prestige = -50
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = king
				}
				prestige = -100
			}
		}
	}
}

					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = count
				}
				prestige = -25
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = duke
				}
				prestige = -50
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = king
				}
				prestige = -100
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_116"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_110" #Then we go to war!
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
				leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_religious_king
				leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_republican_king
				leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_court_king
				leads_faction = faction_court_duke
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 0.49 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				NOT = { liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 0.74 } } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.49 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5.0
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100.0
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 2.99 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				trait = craven
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.204 } #vote
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
				change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
				change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 4 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { real_tier = KING }
				change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 8 }
			}
		}
		character_event = { id = PlusFaction.172 days = 7 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900737 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_110" #Do nothing
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.49 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01
				liege = { check_variable = { which = "rebel_power" value = 1.99 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king

			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = count
				}

			}

				limit = {
					tier = duke
				}
				prestige = -50
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tier = king
				}
				prestige = -100
			}
		}
	}

### FACTION LEADER IS OUSTED

# Faction leader is ousted after wasting a meeting
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.120
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_120"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	immediate = {
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.127 } #notify
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "CURSES"
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -400
		}
	}
}

				tier = king
			}

		}
	}

### MEETING AGENDAS & SPEECHES

# Agenda - strengthen self
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.130
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_130"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_130"	# praise self in speech
		tooltip_info = diplomacy
		trigger = {
			diplomacy = 8
			NOT = { trait = stutter }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				trait = humble
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			15 = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.135 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900700 } } # great speech
			25 = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.137 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900702 } } # good speech
			30 = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.139 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900704 } } # fair speech
			20 = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.141 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900706 } } # bad speech
			10 = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.143 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900708 } } # laughed out of the room
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_130"	# praise self in speech
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { diplomacy = 8 }
				trait = stutter
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				trait = humble

			35 = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.141 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900706 } } # bad speech
			20 = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.143 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIP1900708 } } # laughed out of the room
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_130"	# request funds for self
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.0
				trait = greedy

				factor = 0.25
				trait = charitable
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }

# Faction leader makes great speech
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.135
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_135"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_135"
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = 200
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = great_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = good_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = okay_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = bad_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = terrible_speech
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = great_speech
				years = 10
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.136 } } #notify
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

				tier = count
			}
			prestige = 25
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = 100
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = great_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = good_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = okay_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = bad_speech
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = terrible_speech
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = good_speech
				years = 10
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.138 } } #notify
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

### VOTE RESULTS

# Faction leader wants money - result of the vote
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.145
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_145"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_145" #vote passed
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { tier = king } ROOT = { wealth = 30 } }
			if = { limit = { tier = duke } ROOT = { wealth = 20 } }
			if = { limit = { tier = count } ROOT = { wealth = 10 } }
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.146 } #notify
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_145" #vote failed
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 } }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.147 } #notify
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 33
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.121 days = 3 } }
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

# Yes vote - notify
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.146
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_146"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "OK"
		if = { limit = { tier = king } wealth = -30 }
		if = { limit = { tier = duke } wealth = -20 }
		if = { limit = { tier = count } wealth = -10 }
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Faction leader succeeded in increasing faction opinion of liege
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.148
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_148"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_148"
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.149 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODPLUS
					hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = 3 } }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = PlusFaction.306 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.150 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODPLUS
					hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = 3 } }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = PlusFaction.306 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.150 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODPLUS
					hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_republican" value = 3 } }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = PlusFaction.306 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.150 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = RELIGIOUSFACTIONMOODPLUS
					hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_religious" value = 3 } }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = PlusFaction.306 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.150 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.155 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
						}
					}
				}
			}

				chance = 75
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.121 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {

							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy

					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}

							has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy

					}

							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry

							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor

							leads_faction = faction_court_duke

							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke

							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry

							}
						}
					}
					AND = {

							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke

					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODMINUS

# Faction leader wants money for liege - result of the vote
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.157
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_157"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_145" #vote passed
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		if = { limit = { tier = king } wealth = -30 }
		if = { limit = { tier = duke } wealth = -20 }
		if = { limit = { tier = count } wealth = -10 }
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke

# Yes vote - notify
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.158
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_158"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "OK"
		if = { limit = { tier = king } wealth = -30 }
		if = { limit = { tier = duke } wealth = -20 }
		if = { limit = { tier = count } wealth = -10 }
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Faction leader wants show of support for liege - result of the vote
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.160
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_160"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_145" #vote passed
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}

# Yes vote - notify
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.161
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_161"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		ai = no
	}

	option = {
		name = "OK"
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = FROM
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Faction leader succeeds in decreasing faction opinion of liege
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.163
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_163"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_163"
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.164 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODMINUS
					hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = -3 } }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = PlusFaction.306 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.165 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = COURTFACTIONMOODMINUS
					hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_court" value = -3 } }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = PlusFaction.306 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.165 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODMINUS
					hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_republican" value = -3 } }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = PlusFaction.306 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.165 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = RELIGIOUSFACTIONMOODMINUS
					hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_religious" value = -3 } }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = PlusFaction.306 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.165 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

	picture = "GFX_evt_council"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

							in_faction = faction_feudal_king

							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
