# Faction leader failed in decreasing liege opinion and increased it instead
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.169
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_169"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_169"
		hidden_tooltip = { 
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.170 } #notify
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_angry
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_angry
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 75
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.121 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_court_unhappy
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						liege = {
							has_character_flag = faction_republican_unhappy
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.121 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_feudal_unhappy
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_court_angry

					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						liege = {
							NOT = {
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_angry
								has_character_flag = faction_religious_unhappy
							}
						}

					AND = {
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke

				chance = 20
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.121 days = 3 } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = {
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = FEUDALFACTIONMOODPLUS
					hidden_tooltip = { change_variable = { which = "faction_mood_feudal" value = 3 } }
					hidden_tooltip = { random_courtier = { limit = { ai = yes } character_event = { id = PlusFaction.306 days = 1 } } }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.171 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke

		}

				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor

					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke

			}
			liege = {

					text = REPUBLICANFACTIONMOODPLUS

					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.171 } } #notify
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

# Faction leader wants to declare war - results of the vote
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.172
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_172"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_172" #we go to war!
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.173 } #notify
			}
		}
		liege = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					set_character_flag = faction_feudal_war
					ROOT = {
						add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } } }
						any_faction_backer = {
							faction = faction_feudal_emperor
							add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = PREV modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } } }
						}
					}
				}
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = cb_faction_overthrow_ruler
					faction = faction_feudal_emperor
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					set_character_flag = faction_feudal_war
					ROOT = {
						add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } } }
						any_faction_backer = {
							faction = faction_feudal_king
							add_trait = rebel hidden_tooltip = { liege = { reverse_opinion = { who = PREV modifier = revolting_against years = 100 } } }
						}
					}
				}
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = cb_faction_overthrow_ruler
					faction = faction_feudal_king
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					set_character_flag = faction_feudal_war
					ROOT = {

							leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = PlusFaction.400 }
				}
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_court_king
							leads_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = PlusFaction.410 }
				}
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_religious_king
							leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = PlusFaction.420 }
				}
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
						OR = {
							leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
							leads_faction = faction_republican_king
							leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = PlusFaction.430 }
				}
				any_vassal = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					character_event = { id = PlusFaction.440 }
				}
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_172" #vote failed and I was removed from power
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 } }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {

				if = {

					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }

					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }

	id = PlusFaction.175
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_175"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king

# Faction leader wants to demand reduction of taxes - results of the vote
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.178
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_178"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_145" #vote passed
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = PlusFaction.363 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = PlusFaction.383 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = PlusFaction.373 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {

							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke

							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}

							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {

							in_faction = faction_religious_king

						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.183 } #notify
			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 50
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.121 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
}

# Faction leader wants to demand a change in levy privilege - results of the vote
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.184
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_184"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_145" #vote passed
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
					leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = PlusFaction.364 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_republican_king
					leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = PlusFaction.384 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_religious_king
					leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = PlusFaction.374 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
					leads_faction = faction_court_king
					leads_faction = faction_court_duke
				}
			}
			liege = { letter_event = { id = PlusFaction.353 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPULTIMATUM days = 3 } }
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {

				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {

							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {

							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.188 } #notify
			}
		}
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_postponed
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_145" #vote failed
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 } }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }

				}

				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king

						}

							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }

						}
					}
				}

			}
		}
		random = {
			chance = 50
			custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
			hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = PlusFaction.121 days = 3 } }

# Faction members propose a no confidence vote to oust leader
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.190
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_190"
	
	only_rulers = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
		has_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_meeting_begun }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge }
		NOT = { has_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge_defeated }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { prestige = 0 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { diplomacy = 10 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			diplomacy = 20
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { prestige = 500 }
			any_faction_backer = {
				prestige = 500
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { prestige = 1000 }
			any_faction_backer = {
				prestige = 1000
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { prestige = 2000 }
			any_faction_backer = {
				prestige = 2000
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			OR = {
				leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
				leads_faction = faction_religious_king
				leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			}
			NOT = { piety = 0 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_faction_backer = {
				higher_tier_than = ROOT
				OR = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
						in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
						in_faction = faction_republican_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
						in_faction = faction_republican_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
						in_faction = faction_religious_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
						in_faction = faction_religious_duke
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
						in_faction = faction_court_emperor
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
						in_faction = faction_court_king
					}
					AND = {
						ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
						in_faction = faction_court_duke
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_character_flag = faction_meeting_called
		set_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_190" #go ahead with the vote
		ai_chance = { factor = 90 }
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP44 }
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.200 } #vote
			}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
				change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
				change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -4 }

				change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -8 }
			}

			character_event = { id = PlusFaction.191 days = 7 }
		}
	}
	option = {

				trait = content
			}

				factor = 5
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				trait = proud
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {

			}

			}

			}

		}
		hidden_tooltip = {

							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}

							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}

# Results of the no cofidence vote
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.191
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_191"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_from = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_character_flag = former_faction_leader }
		NOT = { trait = rebel }
		NOT = { trait = loyalist }
		OR = {
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_king
			leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke
			leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_religious_king
			leads_faction = faction_religious_duke
			leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_republican_king
			leads_faction = faction_republican_duke
			leads_faction = faction_court_emperor
			leads_faction = faction_court_king
			leads_faction = faction_court_duke
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_191" #vote passes
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 }
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP45 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = count
			}
			prestige = -100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = duke
			}
			prestige = -200
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier = king
			}
			prestige = -400
		}
		set_character_flag = former_faction_leader
		set_character_flag = removed_from_leadership
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.193 } #notify
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_191" #leadership retained
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0.5 } }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			set_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 0 }
		}
		clr_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge
		set_character_flag = faction_leadership_challenge_defeated
		set_character_flag = faction_meeting
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					OR = {
						reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting }
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP47D }
				}
			}
		}
		liege = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { had_character_flag = { flag = last_vote days = 30 } }
					reverse_has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = BARON }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46A }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46B }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46C }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { real_tier = KING }
					custom_tooltip = { text = CUSTOMTOOLTIP46D }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_faction_backer = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_king }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_feudal_duke }
							in_faction = faction_feudal_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_republican_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_king }
							in_faction = faction_republican_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_republican_duke }
							in_faction = faction_republican_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_religious_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_king }
							in_faction = faction_religious_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_religious_duke }
							in_faction = faction_religious_duke
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_emperor }
							in_faction = faction_court_emperor
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_king }
							in_faction = faction_court_king
						}
						AND = {
							ROOT = { leads_faction = faction_court_duke }
							in_faction = faction_court_duke
						}
					}
				}
				character_event = { id = PlusFaction.194 } #notify
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		ai = no
	}

	option = {
		name = "OK"
	}
}

# Faction member votes on whether to oust leader
character_event = {
	id = PlusFaction.200
	picture = "GFX_evt_council"
	desc = "EVTDESC_PlusFaction_200"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA_PlusFaction_200" #vote yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				lower_tier_than = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 10
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 20
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 30
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 40
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 60
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 70
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				opinion = {
					who = FROM
					value = 80
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = kind
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			ROOT = { set_character_flag = last_vote }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = BARON } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = COUNT } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 2 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = DUKE } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 4 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = KING } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = 8 }
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB_PlusFaction_200" #vote no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				higher_tier_than = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = -10
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = -20
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = -30
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = -40
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					opinion = {
						who = FROM
						value = -50
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				trait = envious
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			ROOT = { set_character_flag = last_vote }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = BARON } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = COUNT } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -2 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = DUKE } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -4 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = KING } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -8 }
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = DUKE } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -4 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { real_tier = KING } }
					change_variable = { which = "faction_votes" value = -8 }
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				}
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_supported_in_meeting
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_opposed_in_meeting
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}
